  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,-->,[['[...]',['$M']]]],T1],[[S,<->,M],T2]],[[P,-->,[['[...]',['$S']]]],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($P --> 
        ( [ $M ])) $T1) 
            ( ($S <-> $M) $T2)) 
            ( ($P --> 
                ( [ $S ])) 
                    (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[['{...}',['$A']],<->,['{...}',['$B']]]],[A,<->,B],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( { $A } <-> 
          { $B })) 
            ($A <-> $B) 
            (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[['[...]',['$A']]],<->,[['[...]',['$B']]]]],[A,<->,B],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ( [ $A ]) <-> 
            ( [ $B ]))) 
                ($A <-> $B) 
                (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))

;;;!Extensional and intensional intersection composition: (sets via reductions)
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,-->,M],T1],[[S,-->,M],T2]],[[[P,'|',S],-->,M],['Truth_Intersection',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($P --> $M) $T1) 
    ( ($S --> $M) $T2)) 
  ( ( ($P | $S) --> $M) 
    (Truth_Intersection $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,-->,M],T1],[[S,-->,M],T2]],[[[P,&,S],-->,M],['Truth_Union',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($P --> $M) $T1) 
    ( ($S --> $M) $T2)) 
  ( ( ($P & $S) --> $M) 
    (Truth_Union $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[P,-->,M],T1],[[S,-->,M],T2]],[[[P,~,S],-->,M],['Truth_Difference',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($P --> $M) $T1) 
    ( ($S --> $M) $T2)) 
  ( ( ($P ~ $S) --> $M) 
    (Truth_Difference $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,P],T1],[[M,-->,S],T2]],[[M,-->,[P,&,S]],['Truth_Intersection',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($M --> $P) $T1) 
    ( ($M --> $S) $T2)) 
  ( ($M --> 
      ($P & $S)) 
    (Truth_Intersection $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,P],T1],[[M,-->,S],T2]],[[M,-->,[P,'|',S]],['Truth_Union',T1,T2]]])

  (|- 
    ( ($M --> $P) $T1) 
    ( ($M --> $S) $T2)) 
  ( ($M --> 
      ($P | $S)) 
    (Truth_Union $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[M,-->,P],T1],[[M,-->,S],T2]],[[M,-->,[P,-,S]],['Truth_Difference',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($M --> $P) $T1) 
    ( ($M --> $S) $T2)) 
  ( ($M --> 
      ($P - $S)) 
    (Truth_Difference $T1 $T2)))


;;;!Extensional and intensional intersection decomposition:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[S,-->,M],T1],[[[S,'|',P],-->,M],T2]],[[P,-->,M],['Truth_DecomposePNN',T1,T2]]])

;;; NAL-4
;;;!Transformation rules between product and image:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T]],[[A,-->,[R,'/1',B]],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T)) 
  ( ($A --> 
      ($R /1 $B)) 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T]],[[B,-->,[R,'/2',A]],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T)) 
  ( ($B --> 
      ($R /2 $A)) 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T]],[[[R,'\\1',B],-->,A],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $B)) $T)) 
  ( ( ($R \1 $B) --> $A) 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T]],[[[R,'\\2',A],-->,B],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $B)) $T)) 
  ( ( ($R \2 $A) --> $B) 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


;;;other direction of same rules (as these are bi-directional)
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,-->,[R,'/1',B]],T]],[[[A,*,B],-->,R],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])

    ( ($A --> 
        ($R /1 $B)) $T)) 
  ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[B,-->,[R,'/2',A]],T]],[[[A,*,B],-->,R],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($B --> 
        ($R /2 $A)) $T)) 
  ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[R,'\\1',B],-->,A],T]],[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($R \1 $B) --> $A) $T)) 
  ( ($R --> 
      ($A * $B)) 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[R,'\\2',A],-->,B],T]],[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])

  (|- 
    ( ( ($R \2 $A) --> $B) $T)) 
  ( ($R --> 
      ($A * $B)) 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


;;;!Comparative relations
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[['{...}',['$R']],'|-',>,[['[...]',['$P']]]],T1],[[['{...}',['$S']],'|-',>,[['[...]',['$P']]]],T2]],[[[['{...}',['$R']],*,['{...}',['$S']]],-->,[>>>,P]],['Truth_FrequencyGreater',T1,T2]]])

          ( [ $P ])) $T1)

                    ( [ $P ])) $T2))

                                { $S }) --> 
                                  (>>> $P))

      (>>> $P)) 
    (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[['{...}',['$R']],'|-',>,[['[...]',['$P']]]],T1],[[['{...}',['$S']],'|-',>,[['[...]',['$P']]]],T2]],[[[['{...}',['$R']],*,['{...}',['$S']]],-->,[===,P]],['Truth_FrequencyEqual',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( { $R } |- > 
          ( [ $P ])) $T1) 
              ( ( { $S } |- > 
                    ( [ $P ])) $T2)) 
                        ( ( ( { $R } * 
                                { $S }) --> 
                                  (=== $P)) 
                                  (Truth_FrequencyEqual $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,[===,P]],T1],[[[B,*,C],-->,[===,P]],T2]],[[[A,*,C],-->,[===,P]],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
(=

      (=== $P))

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,[===,P]],T]],[[[B,*,A],-->,[===,P]],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',T]]])

      (=== $P)) 
    (Truth_StructuralIntersection $T)))


;;;!Optional rules for more efficient reasoning about relation components:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[[C,*,B],-->,R],T2]],[[C,-->,A],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1)

  ( ($C --> $A) 
    (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[[A,*,C],-->,R],T2]],[[C,-->,B],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[C,-->,A],T2]],[[[C,*,B],-->,R],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])

    ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
    ( ($C --> $A) $T2))

    (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[A,-->,C],T2]],[[[C,*,B],-->,R],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
    ( ($A --> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ( ($C * $B) --> $R) 
    (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[C,<->,A],T2]],[[[C,*,B],-->,R],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
    ( ($C <-> $A) $T2)) 
  ( ( ($C * $B) --> $R) 
    (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[C,-->,B],T2]],[[[A,*,C],-->,R],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
    ( ($C --> $B) $T2)) 
  ( ( ($A * $C) --> $R) 
    (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[B,-->,C],T2]],[[[A,*,C],-->,R],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
    ( ($B --> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ( ($A * $C) --> $R) 
    (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[C,<->,B],T2]],[[[A,*,C],-->,R],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
    ( ($C <-> $B) $T2)) 
  ( ( ($A * $C) --> $R) 
    (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[A,-->,C],T2]],[[R,-->,[C,*,B]],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $B)) $T1) 
    ( ($A --> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ($R --> 
      ($C * $B)) 
    (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[C,-->,A],T2]],[[R,-->,[C,*,B]],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])

    ( ($C --> $A) $T2)) 
  ( ($R --> 
      ($C * $B)) 
    (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[C,<->,A],T2]],[[R,-->,[C,*,B]],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $B)) $T1) 
    ( ($C <-> $A) $T2)) 
  ( ($R --> 
      ($C * $B)) 
    (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[B,-->,C],T2]],[[R,-->,[A,*,C]],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $B)) $T1) 
    ( ($B --> $C) $T2)) 
  ( ($R --> 
      ($A * $C)) 
    (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[C,-->,B],T2]],[[R,-->,[A,*,C]],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $B)) $T1) 
    ( ($C --> $B) $T2)) 
  ( ($R --> 
      ($A * $C)) 
    (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[C,<->,B],T2]],[[R,-->,[A,*,C]],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $B)) $T1) 
    ( ($C <-> $B) $T2)) 
  ( ($R --> 
      ($A * $C)) 
    (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[[C,*,B],-->,R],T2]],[[A,<->,C],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
    ( ( ($C * $B) --> $R) $T2)) 
  ( ($A <-> $C) 
    (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[[A,*,C],-->,R],T2]],[[B,<->,C],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
    ( ( ($A * $C) --> $R) $T2)) 
  ( ($B <-> $C) 
    (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[R,-->,[C,*,B]],T2]],[[A,<->,C],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|- 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $B)) $T1) 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($C * $B)) $T2)) 
  ( ($A <-> $C) 
    (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[R,-->,[A,*,C]],T2]],[[B,<->,C],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]]])
(= 
  (|-

        ($A * $B)) $T1) 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $C)) $T2)) 
  ( ($B <-> $C)

;;;!Conditional composition for conjunction and disjunction:
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,C],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[[A,&&,B],==>,C],['Truth_Union',T1,T2]]])

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['|-',[[A,==>,C],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[[A,'||',B],==>,C],['Truth_Intersection',T1,T2]]])

      ($A || $B))

            ( [ $A $B ]))

            ( [ (Cons  $A $B) $C ]))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[[['[...]',[A]]],&,[['[...]',[B,C]]]],[['[...]',[A,[B|C]]]]])

  ( ( [ $A ]) & 
        ( [ $B $C ])) 
            ( [ $A 
                (Cons  $B $C) ]))

; Execution took 0.000059 secs. (58.84 microseconds) 
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['BestCandidate','$VAR'(tuple),'$VAR'(evaluateCandidateFunction),T],[sequential,[[do,['change-state!','&tempbestscore',0]],[do,['change-state!','&tempbest','Nil']],[do,['let*',[['$VAR'(x),[superpose,'$VAR'(tuple)]],['$VAR'(fx),['$VAR'(evaluateCandidateFunction),'$VAR'(x),T]]],[superpose,[['If',[>,'$VAR'(fx),['get-state','&tempbestscore']],[sequential,[['change-state!','&tempbest','$VAR'(x)],['change-state!','&tempbestscore','$VAR'(fx)]]]]]]]],['get-state','&tempbest']]]])

  (sequential 
    ( (do 
        (change-state! &tempbestscore 0)) 
      (do

        (let* 
          ( ($x 
              (superpose $tuple))

              ($evaluateCandidateFunction $x $T)))

            ( (If 
                (> $fx 
                  (get-state &tempbestscore)) 
                (sequential 
                  ( (change-state! &tempbest $x) 
                    (change-state! &tempbestscore $fx)))))))) 
      (get-state &tempbest))))

;;bound the size of the attentional focus for tasks / events
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['BoundEvents','$VAR'(collection),Threshold,Increment,TargetAmount,T],[sequential,[[do,['let*',[[Ev,['get-atoms','$VAR'(collection)]],[['Event',Sentence,[Time,Evidence,EPrio]],Ev]],['If',[<,['EventPriorityNow',EPrio,T],Threshold],['remove-atom','$VAR'(collection),Ev]]]],[let,CurrentAmount,['CollapseCardinality',['get-atoms','$VAR'(collection)]],['If',[>,CurrentAmount,TargetAmount],['BoundEvents','$VAR'(collection),[+,Threshold,Increment],Increment,TargetAmount,T]]]]]])
(= 
  (BoundEvents $collection $Threshold $Increment $TargetAmount $T) 
  (sequential 
    ( (do 
        (let* 
          ( ($Ev 
              (get-atoms $collection)) 
            ( (Event $Sentence 
                ($Time $Evidence $EPrio)) $Ev)) 
          (If 
            (< 
              (EventPriorityNow $EPrio $T) $Threshold) 
            (remove-atom $collection $Ev)))) 
      (let $CurrentAmount 
        (CollapseCardinality 
          (get-atoms $collection)) 
        (If 
          (> $CurrentAmount $TargetAmount) 
          (BoundEvents $collection 
            (+ $Threshold $Increment) $Increment $TargetAmount $T))))))

;;;update beliefs in existing concept with the new event or create new concept to enter the new evidence
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['UpdateConcept',NewEvent,T],['let*',[[['Event',[Term,TV],[Time,Evidence,EPrio]],NewEvent],[NewEventEternalized,['Eternalize',NewEvent]],[MatchConcept,['Concept',Term,Belief,BeliefEvent,CPrio]]],[sequential,[[case,[match,'&attentional_focus',MatchConcept,MatchConcept],[[MatchConcept,[sequential,[['remove-atom','&attentional_focus',MatchConcept],['let*',[[RevisedBelief,['RevisionAndChoice',Belief,NewEventEternalized]],[MaxPrio,['If',[>,['EventPriorityNow',EPrio,T],['ConceptPriorityNow',CPrio,T]],EPrio,CPrio]]],['add-atom','&attentional_focus',['Concept',Term,RevisedBelief,NewEvent,MaxPrio]]]]]],['%void%',[case,[match,'&concepts',MatchConcept,MatchConcept],[[MatchConcept,[sequential,[['remove-atom','&concepts',MatchConcept],['add-atom','&attentional_focus',MatchConcept],['UpdateConcept',NewEvent,T]]]],['%void%',['add-atom','&attentional_focus',['Concept',Term,NewEventEternalized,NewEvent,EPrio]]]]]]]]]]]])

      ( (case 
          (match &attentional_focus $MatchConcept $MatchConcept) 
          ( ($MatchConcept 
              (sequential 
                ( (remove-atom &attentional_focus $MatchConcept) 
                  (let* 
                    ( ($RevisedBelief 
                        (RevisionAndChoice $Belief $NewEventEternalized)) 
                      ($MaxPrio

                          (> 
                            (EventPriorityNow $EPrio $T) 
                            (ConceptPriorityNow $CPrio $T)) $EPrio $CPrio)))

                      (Concept $Term $RevisedBelief $NewEvent $MaxPrio))))))

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['Execute',Opname],[superpose,[['AddBeliefEvent',[Opname,[1.0,0.9]]],Opname]]])

  (Execute $Opname)

    ( (AddBeliefEvent 
        ($Opname 
          (1.0 0.9))) $Opname)))


;;Add subgoals to the PQ
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['DeriveSubgoals',Options],[do,[let,['Decision',Op,Subgoal],[superpose,Options],['add-atom','&goal_events',Subgoal]]]])

  (do

      (Decision $Op $Subgoal)

;;execute the operation which most likely gets the goal achieved in current contexts, and if contexts are not yet fulfilled, derive them as subgoals
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['BestDecision',T,['Event',[Term,DV],[GoalTime,GoalEvBase,GoalPrio]],FIFO],[let,Options,[collapse,['let*',[[['Event',[[[Prec,&/,[^,Op]],=/>,Term],ImpTV],[ImpTime,ImpEvBase,ImpPrio]],['EternalQuestion',[[Prec,&/,[^,Op]],=/>,Term]]],[DVPrecOp,['Truth_Deduction',DV,ImpTV]],[['Event',[PrecTerm,PrecTV],PrecMetadata],['Projection',['EventQuestion',Prec],T]],[DVOp,['Truth_Deduction',PrecTV,DVPrecOp]],[DVPrec,['Truth_StructuralDeduction',DVPrecOp]],[SubgoalStamp,['TupleConcat',GoalEvBase,ImpEvBase]]],['If',['StampDisjoint',SubgoalStamp],['Decision',[[^,Op],DVOp],['Event',[Prec,['Truth_StructuralDeduction',DVPrecOp]],[T,SubgoalStamp,[T,['SubgoalPriority',['EventPriorityNow',GoalPrio,T],DVPrec]]]]]]]],[let,['Decision',[Opname,DVOp],Subgoal],['BestCandidate',Options,'OpExpectation',T],['If',[>,['Truth_Expectation',DVOp],0.5],['Execute',Opname],['DeriveSubgoals',Options]]]]])
(= 
  (BestDecision $T 
    (Event 
      ($Term $DV) 
      ($GoalTime $GoalEvBase $GoalPrio)) $FIFO) 
  (let $Options 
    (collapse 
      (let* 
        ( ( (Event 
              ( ( ($Prec &/ 
                    (^ $Op)) =/> $Term) $ImpTV) 
              ($ImpTime $ImpEvBase $ImpPrio)) 
            (EternalQuestion 
              ( ($Prec &/ 
                  (^ $Op)) =/> $Term))) 
          ($DVPrecOp 
            (Truth_Deduction $DV $ImpTV)) 
          ( (Event 
              ($PrecTerm $PrecTV) $PrecMetadata) 
            (Projection 
              (EventQuestion $Prec) $T)) 
          ($DVOp 
            (Truth_Deduction $PrecTV $DVPrecOp)) 
          ($DVPrec 
            (Truth_StructuralDeduction $DVPrecOp)) 
          ($SubgoalStamp 
            (TupleConcat $GoalEvBase $ImpEvBase))) 
        (If 
          (StampDisjoint $SubgoalStamp) 
          (Decision 
            ( (^ $Op) $DVOp) 
            (Event 
              ($Prec 
                (Truth_StructuralDeduction $DVPrecOp)) 
              ($T $SubgoalStamp 
                ($T 
                  (SubgoalPriority 
                    (EventPriorityNow $GoalPrio $T) $DVPrec)))))))) 
    (let 
      (Decision 
        ($Opname $DVOp) $Subgoal) 
      (BestCandidate $Options OpExpectation $T) 
      (If 
        (> 
          (Truth_Expectation $DVOp) 0.5) 
        (Execute $Opname) 
        (DeriveSubgoals $Options)))))


;;;select the highest priority goal event from the PQ and use it for decision making
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['GoalCycle',T],[sequential,[[let,Ev,['SelectHighestPriorityEvent','&goal_events',T],[sequential,[[do,['remove-atom','&goal_events',Ev]],['BestDecision',T,Ev,['get-state','&FIFO']]]]],[do,['UpdateReasonerState']],[do,['BoundEvents','&goal_events',0.0,0.1,['GoalEventsMax'],T]]]]])
(= 
  (GoalCycle $T) 
  (sequential 
    ( (let $Ev 
        (SelectHighestPriorityEvent &goal_events $T) 
        (sequential 
          ( (do 
              (remove-atom &goal_events $Ev)) 
            (BestDecision $T $Ev 
              (get-state &FIFO))))) 
      (do 
        (UpdateReasonerState)) 
      (do 
        (BoundEvents &goal_events 0.0 0.1 
          (GoalEventsMax) $T)))))


;;;Input procedure
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['AddGoalEvent',Sentence],['let*',[[[T,'$VAR'(evidentialBase)],['GetReasonerState']],[InputEvent,['Event',Sentence,[T,'$VAR'(evidentialBase),[T,1.0]]]]],[sequential,[[do,['add-atom','&goal_events',InputEvent]],['GoalCycle',T]]]]])
(=

          ($T $evidentialBase 
            ($T 1.0)))))

        (GoalCycle $T)))))
